# <a name="office-365-germany"></a><span data-ttu-id="93edf-104">Office 365 德國</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-104">Office 365 Germany</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93edf-105">Office 365 德國是一種可在歐洲使用的 Office 365 服務的區別選項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-105">Office 365 Germany is a differentiated option from the Office 365 services already available across Europe.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-106">它可透過以德國法律為依據的獨特資料受信者模型，為數字工作、歐盟（歐盟）和歐洲免費交易協會（EFTA）提供業界領先的工作效率服務，以協助滿足在德國、歐盟（EU）和歐洲免費交易協會（）中最受管制客戶的需求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-106">It helps address the needs of the most regulated customers in Germany, the European Union (EU), and the European Free Trade Association (EFTA) by delivering our industry-leading productivity services for digital work, from German data centers, with data residency in Germany and strict data access and control measures via a unique data trustee model governed under German law.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93edf-p103">資料信任者 T-Systems International (獨立德國公司) 和 Deutsche Telekom 子公司會控制客戶資料的實體和邏輯存取。非由資料信任者 (德國法律所規範) 核准或監督不得存取客戶資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-p103">The data trustee, T-Systems International, an independent German company and subsidiary of Deutsche Telekom, controls physical and logical access to customer data. Customer data cannot be accessed without approval from or supervision by the data trustee, which is governed by German law.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93edf-109">根據客戶的需求，我們的雲端策略會將重點放在德國中與我們的全球雲端產品一致的新雲端地區。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-109">Based on this evolution in customers' needs, our cloud strategy for Germany will focus on delivery of the new cloud regions in Germany that are consistent with our global cloud offering.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-110">透過這個重點，我們將不再接受新的客戶，或從目前可用的 Microsoft 雲端德國部署任何新的服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-110">With this focus, we will no longer be accepting new customers or deploying any new services from the currently available Microsoft Cloud Germany.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-111">現有的客戶可以繼續使用目前的雲端服務，我們會使用必要的安全性更新加以維護。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-111">Existing customers can continue to use the current cloud services available today, which we'll maintain with necessary security updates.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-112">[深入瞭解 Office 365 德國](https://support.office.com/article/Learn-about-Office-365-Germany-8a5a4bbc-667a-4cac-8769-d8ac9015db4c?ui=en-US&amp;rs=en-US&amp;ad=US)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-112">[Learn about Office 365 Germany](https://support.office.com/article/Learn-about-Office-365-Germany-8a5a4bbc-667a-4cac-8769-d8ac9015db4c?ui=en-US&amp;rs=en-US&amp;ad=US).</span></span>

## <a name="service-availability-for-each-plan"></a><span data-ttu-id="93edf-113">每個方案可用的服務</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-113">Service availability for each plan</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93edf-p105">每個 Office 365 Germany 方案皆包含一些個別服務，例如 Exchange Online 和 SharePoint Online。下表顯示每項 Office 365 方案中可用的服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-p105">Each Office 365 Germany plan includes a number of individual services, such as Exchange Online and SharePoint Online. The following table shows the services that are available in each Office 365 plan.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-233"><sup>1</sup>雲端式訂閱服務與相關的功能，包括 Microsoft 365 系統管理中心，您可以在這裡設定使用者和網域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-233"><sup>1</sup> Cloud-based subscription service with related features including the Microsoft 365 admin center where you can set up users and domains.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-234"><sup>2</sup> 您可以單獨購買 Office 365 專業增強版 計劃。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-234"><sup>2</sup> You can buy an Office 365 ProPlus plan separately.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-235">Office 365 專業增強版 隨附於 Office 365 Germany 企業版 E3 和 Office 365 Germany 企業版 E4。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-235">Office 365 ProPlus is included with Office 365 Germany Enterprise E3 and Office 365 Germany Enterprise E4.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-236">[必須啟用新式驗證](https://support.office.com/article/modern-authentication-be-enabled-776c0036-66fd-41cb-8928-5495c0f9168a)，才能搭配 Office 365 Germany 使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-236">[Modern authentication](https://support.office.com/article/modern-authentication-be-enabled-776c0036-66fd-41cb-8928-5495c0f9168a) must be enabled for use with Office 365 Germany.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-237"><sup>3</sup> Project Online 和 Power BI 並不包含在內，但可以當做附加服務來單獨購買，若是 Office 365 Germany 教育版 A1 方案，則可免費新增此功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-237"><sup>3</sup> Project Online and Power BI are not included, but can be purchased as a separate add-on service or added for free to the Office 365 Germany Education A1 plan.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-238"><sup>4</sup>可免費使用 web 用的 Visio （view 功能）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-238"><sup>4</sup> Visio for the web consumption (view capability) is available for free.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-239">Visio 網頁版建立和編輯功能需要授權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-239">Visio for the web create and edit capabilities require a license.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-240">如需有關 web Visio 的詳細資訊，請參閱[visio for web service description](../visio-online-service-description/visio-online-service-description.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-240">For more information about Visio for the web, see the [Visio for the web service description](../visio-online-service-description/visio-online-service-description.md).</span></span>

## <a name="security-amp-compliance-center-availability-in-office-365-germany"></a><span data-ttu-id="93edf-243">Security &amp; Compliance Center availability in Office 365 Germany</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-243">Security &amp; Compliance Center availability in Office 365 Germany</span></span>

### <a name="what-compliance-certificates-are-provided-for-office-365-germany"></a><span data-ttu-id="93edf-246">Office 365 德國所提供的相容性憑證為何？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-246">What compliance certificates are provided for Office 365 Germany?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93edf-247">Office 365 德國遵循 Office 365 的雲端安全性和符合性標準。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-247">Office 365 Germany adheres to the cloud security and compliance standards of Office 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-248">Office 365 提供一組完整的認證，可獨立評估，以作為服務組織控制（SOC）、國際標準組織（ISO）和審核的一部分，由已獲得資格的審計員進行評估。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-248">Office 365 offers a comprehensive set of certifications, independently assessed by accredited auditors as part of Service Organization Controls (SOC), International Organization for Standardization (ISO), and audits.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-249">認證包括 ISO 27001/27002、27017、27018和 SOC 1 和2。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-249">The certifications include ISO 27001/27002, 27017, 27018, and SOC 1 and 2.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-250">Office 365 Germany 中其他的資料受託人控制，則會由獨立人士進行評估，是我們每年 ISO 和 SOC 稽核的一環。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-250">The additional data trustee controls in Office 365 Germany will be evaluated by independent assessors as part of our annual ISO and SOC audits.</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-1649"><sup>1</sup> Office 365 德國方案包括用戶端軟體應用程式，已在使用者的裝置上安裝及執行（「用戶端軟體應用程式」），例如 office 365 ProPlus、office 2013 和 office 2016。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1649"><sup>1</sup> Office 365 Germany plans include client software applications that are installed and run on an end-user's device ("client software applications"), such as Office 365 ProPlus, Office 2013, and Office 2016.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-1650">用戶端軟體應用程式不會以獨佔方式在德國資料中心內運作，並可讓使用者存取非德文線上服務的線上服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1650">Client software applications do not operate exclusively in German data centers and may let an end-user access online services that are not German Online Services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-1651">為了與 Microsoft 的協議，用戶端軟體應用程式不是 German Online Services。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1651">For purposes of your agreement with Microsoft, client software applications are not German Online Services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-1652">德國資料落地承諾和德國資料受託人的存取控制僅適用於 German Online Services。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1652">German data residency commitments and access control by German data trustee apply only to the German Online Services.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-1653"><sup>2</sup> Office 2013 需要 [modern authentication be enabled](https://support.office.com/article/Using-Office-365-modern-authentication-with-Office-clients-776c0036-66fd-41cb-8928-5495c0f9168a?ui=en-US&amp;rs=en-US&amp;ad=US&amp;fromAR=1)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1653"><sup>2</sup> Office 2013 requires that [modern authentication be enabled](https://support.office.com/article/Using-Office-365-modern-authentication-with-Office-clients-776c0036-66fd-41cb-8928-5495c0f9168a?ui=en-US&amp;rs=en-US&amp;ad=US&amp;fromAR=1).</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-1654"><sup>3</sup> Azure 資訊保護未包含在內，但能以個別的附加元件形式購買，才能啟用支援的 IRM 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1654"><sup>3</sup> Azure Information Protection is not included but can be purchased as a separate add-on in order to enable the supported IRM features.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-1655"><sup>4</sup> Windows Server AD RMS 是內部部署伺服器，必須個別採購並管理，以便啟用支援的 IRM 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1655"><sup>4</sup> Windows Server AD RMS is an on-premises server that must be purchased and managed separately in order to enable the supported IRM features.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-1656"><sup>5</sup> 如果您有 Office Professional Plus 2013 或獨立版本的 Excel 2013，則可以下載 [Power Map Preview for Excel 2013](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=397382&amp;clcid=0x409) 並將之做為不受支援的增益集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1656"><sup>5</sup> If you have Office Professional Plus 2013 or a standalone version of Excel 2013, you can download and use the [Power Map Preview for Excel 2013](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=397382&amp;clcid=0x409) as an unsupported add-in.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-1657"><sup>6</sup>商務用 Skype Basic 適用于所有客戶。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1657"><sup>6</sup> Skype for Business Basic is available for all customers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-1658">商務用 Skype 桌面用戶端是在本機安裝的應用程式，可針對包含 商務用 Skype Online 的 Office 365 方案，提供目前狀態、立即訊息和會議功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1658">The Skype for Business desktop client is a locally installed application that provides presence, instant messaging, and conferencing features for Office 365 plans that include Skype for Business Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-1659">Office 365 專業增強版 和 Office 365 Germany 企業版 E3 包含完整的 Skype 應用程式，其包含額外的功能，例如：進階電話語音支援、封存和法規遵循功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1659">Office 365 ProPlus, and Office 365 Germany Enterprise E3 include the full Skype application, which includes additional features including advanced telephony support, archiving, and compliance features.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-1660">必須為每個使用者指派商務用 Skype Online 授權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1660">A Skype for Business Online license must be assigned for each user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-1661">如需 Lync Basic 功能的詳細資訊，請參閱[Dektop client comparison tables](https://docs.microsoft.com/lyncserver/lync-server-2013-desktop-client-comparison-tables)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1661">For more information on Lync Basic features, see [Dektop client comparison tables](https://docs.microsoft.com/lyncserver/lync-server-2013-desktop-client-comparison-tables).</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-1662"><sup>7</sup> 部分學校符合 Education Plus 的資格，其包含 Office 365 專業增強版，可讓學生和教職員在最多五部 PC 或 Mac 電腦及其他行動裝置 (包含 Windows 平版電腦及 iPad) 上安裝最新版的 Office。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1662"><sup>7</sup> Some schools are eligible for Education Plus, which includes Office 365 ProPlus, and allows students, faculty and staff to install the latest version of Office on up to five PC or Mac computers and on other mobile devices, including Windows tablets and the iPad.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-1663">當學校透過註冊教育版解決方案、Open Value Subscription 教育版解決方案或學校合約，為全機構的教職人員授權 Office 時，學校即符合 Office 365 教育增強版的資格。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1663">Schools qualify for Office 365 Education Plus when they license Office institution-wide for faculty and staff through Enrollment for Education Solutions, Open Value Subscription Education Solutions, or a school contract.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-1664">請注意，Access 和 Publisher 僅在 PC 上可供使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1664">Note that Access and Publisher are available on PCs only.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-1665">OneNote for Mac 可分別從 Mac App Store 下載。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1665">OneNote for Mac is available as a separate download from the Mac App Store.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-1666"><sup>8</sup> 可安裝 Office 2011 for Mac，但不可啟用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1666"><sup>8</sup> Office 2011 for Mac can be installed, but not activated.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-1667"><sup>9</sup>Office 365 Germany 企業版 E3 和 Office 365 專業增強版 的大量授權啟動限於在 Windows Server 2008 R2 與更新版本上的安裝，以及啟用 RDS 角色或 Windows To Go 安裝。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1667"><sup>9</sup> Volume activation for Office 365 Germany Enterprise E3 and Office 365 ProPlus is limited to installations on Windows Server 2008 R2 and newer with the RDS role enabled or Windows To Go installations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-1668">在任一情況中，存取這些安裝的使用者必須為 Office 365 Germany 企業版 E3 或 Office 365 專業增強版 的授權使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1668">In either case, users accessing these installations need to be licensed users of Office 365 Germany Enterprise E3 or Office 365 ProPlus.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-1669"><sup>10</sup>若您是在目前通道或目標發行的延期通道上，則目前可以使用 Access。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1669"><sup>10</sup> Access is currently available if you're on Current Channel or on Targeted release for Deferred Channel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-1670">如果您在順延通道上，則可在 2017 年 6 月存取 Access。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1670">If you're on Deferred Channel, Access will be available in June 2017.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-1671">如需詳細資訊，請參閱＜ [Office 365 商務版和商務進階版中將包含 Access](https://support.office.com/article/Access-included-as-part-of-Office-365-Business-and-Business-Premium-f55c8362-5816-4f8b-897d-0a05e7ba0fef?ui=en-US&amp;rs=en-US&amp;ad=US)＞。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1671">For more information, see [Access included as part of Office 365 Business and Business Premium](https://support.office.com/article/Access-included-as-part-of-Office-365-Business-and-Business-Premium-f55c8362-5816-4f8b-897d-0a05e7ba0fef?ui=en-US&amp;rs=en-US&amp;ad=US).</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-1672"><sup>11</sup>Office 365 Germany 中無法使用，但是即將推出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1672"><sup>11</sup> Not available for Office 365 Germany, but coming soon.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-1866"><sup>1</sup> Office 365 德國方案包括用戶端軟體應用程式，已在使用者的裝置上安裝及執行（「用戶端軟體應用程式」），例如 office 365 ProPlus、office 2013 和 office 2016。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1866"><sup>1</sup> Office 365 Germany plans include client software applications that are installed and run on an end-user's device ("client software applications"), such as Office 365 ProPlus, Office 2013, and Office 2016.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-1867">用戶端軟體應用程式不會以獨佔方式在德國資料中心內運作，並可讓使用者存取非德文線上服務的線上服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1867">Client software applications do not operate exclusively in German data centers and may let an end-user access online services that are not German Online Services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-1868">為了與 Microsoft 的協議，用戶端軟體應用程式不是 German Online Services。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1868">For purposes of your agreement with Microsoft, client software applications are not German Online Services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-1869">德國資料落地承諾和德國資料受託人的存取控制僅適用於 German Online Services。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1869">German data residency commitments and access control by German data trustee apply only to the German Online Services.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-1870"><sup>2</sup> Office 2013 需要 [modern authentication be enabled](https://support.office.com/article/Using-Office-365-modern-authentication-with-Office-clients-776c0036-66fd-41cb-8928-5495c0f9168a?ui=en-US&amp;rs=en-US&amp;ad=US&amp;fromAR=1)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1870"><sup>2</sup> Office 2013 requires that [modern authentication be enabled](https://support.office.com/article/Using-Office-365-modern-authentication-with-Office-clients-776c0036-66fd-41cb-8928-5495c0f9168a?ui=en-US&amp;rs=en-US&amp;ad=US&amp;fromAR=1).</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-1871"><sup>3</sup> 此 Office 版本支援封存和規範功能，但 Exchange Online 和 SharePoint Online 計劃不包含在內，必須另外購買或搭配支援的同等內部部署伺服器使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1871"><sup>3</sup> Archiving and compliance features are supported with this version of Office, but the Exchange Online and SharePoint Online plans are not included and must be purchased separately or used with supported on-premises server equivalents.</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-1872"><sup>4</sup> Azure 資訊保護未包含在內，但能以個別的附加元件形式購買，才能啟用支援的 IRM 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1872"><sup>4</sup> Azure Information Protection is not included but can be purchased as a separate add-on in order to enable the supported IRM features.</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-1873"><sup>5</sup> Windows Server AD RMS 是內部部署伺服器，必須個別採購並管理，以便啟用支援的 IRM 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1873"><sup>5</sup> Windows Server AD RMS is an on-premises server that must be purchased and managed separately in order to enable the supported IRM features.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-1874"><sup>6</sup> 如果您有 Office Professional Plus 2013 或獨立版本的 Excel 2013，則可以下載 [Power Map Preview for Excel 2013](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=397382&amp;clcid=0x409) 並將之做為不受支援的增益集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1874"><sup>6</sup> If you have Office Professional Plus 2013 or a standalone version of Excel 2013, you can download and use the [Power Map Preview for Excel 2013](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=397382&amp;clcid=0x409) as an unsupported add-in.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-1875"><sup>7</sup>商務用 Skype Basic 適用于所有客戶。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1875"><sup>7</sup> Skype for Business Basic is available for all customers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-1876">商務用 Skype 桌面用戶端是在本機安裝的應用程式，可針對包含 商務用 Skype Online 的 Office 365 方案，提供目前狀態、立即訊息和會議功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1876">The Skype for Business desktop client is a locally installed application that provides presence, instant messaging, and conferencing features for Office 365 plans that include Skype for Business Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-1877">Office 365 專業增強版 和 Office 365 Enterprise E3 包含完整的 Skype 應用程式，其包含額外的功能，例如：進階電話語音支援、封存和法規遵循功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1877">Office 365 ProPlus, and Office 365 Enterprise E3 include the full Skype application, which includes additional features including advanced telephony support, archiving, and compliance features.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-1878">必須為每個使用者指派商務用 Skype Online 授權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1878">A Skype for Business Online license must be assigned for each user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-1879">如需有關 Lync 基本功能的詳細資訊，請參閱[桌面用戶端比較表](https://docs.microsoft.com/lyncserver/lync-server-2013-desktop-client-comparison-tables) (英文)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1879">For more information on Lync Basic features, see [Desktop client comparison tables](https://docs.microsoft.com/lyncserver/lync-server-2013-desktop-client-comparison-tables).</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-1880"><sup>8</sup> 可安裝 Office 2011 for Mac，但不可啟用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1880"><sup>8</sup> Office 2011 for Mac can be installed, but not activated.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-1881"><sup>9</sup> Office 365 ProPlus 支援使用者專用的虛擬桌面基礎結構（VDI）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1881"><sup>9</sup> Office 365 ProPlus is supported on user-dedicated virtual desktop infrastructure (VDI).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-1882">當透過大量授權方案購買時，Office 365 專業增強版 僅支援遠端桌面服務 (RDS)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1882">Office 365 ProPlus supports Remote Desktop Services (RDS) only when purchased through a Volume Licensing Program.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-1883"><sup>10</sup>Office 365 Germany 企業版 E3 和 Office 365 專業增強版 的大量授權啟動限於在 Windows Server 2008 R2 與更新版本上的安裝，以及啟用 RDS 角色或 Windows To Go 安裝。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1883"><sup>10</sup> Volume activation for Office 365 Germany Enterprise E3 and Office 365 ProPlus is limited to installations on Windows Server 2008 R2 and newer with the RDS role enabled or Windows To Go installations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-1884">在任一情況中，存取這些安裝的使用者必須為 Office 365 Germany 企業版 E3 或 Office 365 專業增強版 的授權使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1884">In either case, users accessing these installations need to be licensed users of Office 365 Germany Enterprise E3 or Office 365 ProPlus.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-1885"><sup>11</sup>Office 365 Germany 中無法使用，但是即將推出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1885"><sup>11</sup> Not available for Office 365 Germany, but coming soon.</span></span>

## <a name="office-for-the-web-features"></a><span data-ttu-id="93edf-1886">網頁版 Office 的功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1886">Office for the web features</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93edf-1887">下表提供 office 365 德國方案中提供的 web 功能功能的比較連結，以功能豐富的 Microsoft Office 桌面應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1887">The following table provides links to comparisons of Office for the web feature capabilities available in Office 365 Germany plans to feature-rich Microsoft Office desktop apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-1888">使用此比較表了解網頁版 Office 提供的功能，然後選取功能名稱，即可閱讀該功能的簡短描述。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1888">Use the comparisons to discover what features are available in Office for the web and then select the feature name to read a brief description about how that feature works.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-1889">您會發現組織中有些人可能需要使用 Excel 桌面應用程式的進階圖表功能，然而，有些人只需要透過網頁版 Office 來檢視和局部編輯 Word 文件與 PowerPoint 簡報。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1889">You may discover that some people in your organization may need the advanced charting capability of the Excel desktop app while others may only need to view and lightly edit Word documents and PowerPoint presentations with Office for the web.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> - <span data-ttu-id="93edf-1890">Office 桌面套件涵蓋了 Office 的有限精選功能，提供進階功能讓您運用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1890">A limited selection of Office features has been chosen to represent the advanced capabilities of the Office desktop suite.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-1891">此表未完整列出 Microsoft Office 的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1891">The table is not a comprehensive list of Microsoft Office features.</span></span> <br/>
> - <span data-ttu-id="93edf-1892">Microsoft Office 365 專業增強版是最新版 Office 桌面套件推出的每月訂閱產品項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1892">Microsoft Office 365 ProPlus is a monthly subscription offer of the latest Office desktop suite.</span></span> <br/>
> - <span data-ttu-id="93edf-1893">如果內部部署客戶已購買 Office 桌面套件授權（例如： Office Professional Plus、Office Standard 或 Office 365 ProPlus 授權），Microsoft Office Web Apps Server 2013 內部部署客戶便可取得 Web 編輯授權的 Office。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1893">Microsoft Office Web Apps Server 2013 on-premises customers get an Office for the web editing license if they have purchased an Office desktop suite license (such as Office Professional Plus, Office Standard, or an Office 365 ProPlus license).</span></span> <br/>
> - <span data-ttu-id="93edf-1894">由於 Office 365 德國的性質，有些功能尚未啟用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1894">Due to the nature of Office 365 Germany, there are some features that have not yet been enabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-1895">經過一段時間後，您將會看到全球服務所提供的服務功能逐漸完善。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-1895">You will see the services come closer to full feature parity with global services over time.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-2818"><sup>1</sup> Exchange 2010 只支援最低的混合部署。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2818"><sup>1</sup> Exchange 2010 supports only minimal hybrid deployment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-2819">（Exchange 2010 不支援完整混合部署。）如需最低混合部署的詳細資訊，請參閱[使用快速遷移將 Exchange 信箱遷移至 Office 365](https://support.office.com/article/Use-express-migration-to-migrate-Exchange-mailboxes-to-Office-365-fdecceed-0702-4af3-85be-f2a0013937ef?ui=en-US&amp;rs=en-US&amp;ad=US)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2819">(Full hybrid deployment is not supported for Exchange 2010.) For more information about minimal hybrid deployment, see [Use express migration to migrate Exchange mailboxes to Office 365](https://support.office.com/article/Use-express-migration-to-migrate-Exchange-mailboxes-to-Office-365-fdecceed-0702-4af3-85be-f2a0013937ef?ui=en-US&amp;rs=en-US&amp;ad=US).</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-2820"><sup>2</sup> Office 365 德國商務基本版和 Office 365 德國企業版 Premium 不會提供使用內部部署伺服器的使用存取權利。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2820"><sup>2</sup> Office 365 Germany Business Essentials and Office 365 Germany Business Premium do not provide access rights for utilization with on-premises servers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-2821">為了相容，客戶必須購買或已購買適當的 CAL，或升級至提供這些存取權的企業版 SKU。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2821">To be compliant, customer must purchase or have previously purchased the appropriate CALs or upgrade to an Enterprise SKU, which provides these access rights.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-2822"><sup>3</sup>不適用於 Office 365 德國，但即將推出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2822"><sup>3</sup> Not available for Office 365 Germany, but coming soon.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-2823"><sup>4</sup> Azure 資訊保護未包含在內，但能以個別的附加元件形式購買（或免費新增至 Office 365 德國教育版 A1 方案），以便啟用支援的 IRM 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2823"><sup>4</sup> Azure Information Protection is not included but can be purchased as a separate add-on (or added for free to the Office 365 Germany Education A1 plan) in order to enable the supported IRM features.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-2824">Office 365 郵件加密取決於 Azure 資訊保護。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2824">Office 365 Message Encryption depends on Azure Information Protection.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-2825"><sup>5</sup> Windows Server AD RMS 是內部部署伺服器，必須個別採購並管理，以便啟用支援的 IRM 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2825"><sup>5</sup> Windows Server AD RMS is an on-premises server that must be purchased and managed separately in order to enable the supported IRM features.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-2826"><sup>6</sup>對於 eDiscovery，您需要針對內部部署與雲端使用個別查詢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2826"><sup>6</sup> For eDiscovery, you need a separate query for on-premises vs. cloud.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-2827"><sup>7</sup>郵件流程規則（也稱為傳輸規則）是由彈性準則所組成，可讓您根據準則定義要採取的條件、例外狀況和動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2827"><sup>7</sup> Mail flow rules (also known as transport rules) are made up of flexible criteria, which allow you to define conditions, exceptions and actions to take based on the criteria.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-2828">Exchange Online 和 Microsoft Exchange Server 可用的條件、例外狀況和動作各不相同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2828">The available conditions, exceptions, and actions differ between Exchange Online and Microsoft Exchange Server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-2829">如需詳細資訊，請參閱各項產品的對應主題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2829">For more information, see the corresponding topics for each product.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-2830"><sup>8</sup>只能透過直接存取 Exchange 系統管理中心（EAC）管理介面進行存取。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2830"><sup>8</sup> Only accessible via direct access to the Exchange admin center (EAC) management interface.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-2831"><sup>9</sup> Exchange Server 2013 只會使用 Microsoft 反惡意程式碼引擎。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2831"><sup>9</sup> Exchange Server 2013 uses only the Microsoft anti-malware engine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-2832">Exchange Online 使用多個反惡意程式碼引擎，來掃描輸入、輸出和內部訊息中是否有惡意程式碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2832">Exchange Online uses multiple anti-malware engines to scan inbound, outbound, and internal messages for malware.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-2833"><sup>10</sup>已連線的帳戶支援 POP &amp; IMAP 帳戶，但對 Outlook.com （Hotmail）停用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2833"><sup>10</sup> Connected accounts are supported for POP &amp; IMAP accounts, but disabled for Outlook.com (Hotmail).</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-2834"><sup>11</sup>針對需要非使用中信箱功能的信箱，可另外購買 EOA 訂閱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2834"><sup>11</sup> An EOA subscription can be purchased separately for each mailbox that requires the inactive mailbox feature.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-2835"><sup>12</sup>不支援使用 Cmdlet 來使用通訊清單及全域通訊清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2835"><sup>12</sup> Using a cmdlet to work with the Address List and Global Address List is not supported.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-2836"><sup>13</sup>需要使用可用性位址空間來支援與其他承租人共用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2836"><sup>13</sup> Requires using availability address space to support sharing with other tenants.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-2837">如需如何建立可用性位址空間的詳細資訊，請參閱[Add-AvailabilityAddressSpace](https://docs.microsoft.com/powershell/module/exchange/sharing-and-collaboration/Add-AvailabilityAddressSpace?view=exchange-ps)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2837">For more information on how to create an availability address space, see [Add-AvailabilityAddressSpace](https://docs.microsoft.com/powershell/module/exchange/sharing-and-collaboration/Add-AvailabilityAddressSpace?view=exchange-ps).</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-2838"><sup>14</sup>表格指出用戶端是否與相關聯的計畫一起運作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2838"><sup>14</sup> Table indicates whether or not the client works with the associated plans.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-2839">其並不代表這些計劃的採購中必須包含用戶端。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2839">It does not mean the clients are necessarily included in the purchase of these plans.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-2840"><sup>15</sup>支援 POP，但是不支援 IMAP。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2840"><sup>15</sup> POP is supported, but IMAP is not.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-2841"><sup>16</sup>某些協力廠商的 web 元件和增益集可能無法使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2841"><sup>16</sup> Some third-party web parts and add-ins may not be available.</span></span>

## <a name="exchange-online-protection-features"></a><span data-ttu-id="93edf-2842">Exchange Online Protection 功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2842">Exchange Online Protection features</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93edf-2843">下表列出可用於 Office 365 Germany 方案的 Exchange Online Protection (EOP) 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2843">The following table lists the Exchange Online Protection (EOP) features that are available across Office 365 Germany plans.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-2844">如需 EOP 功能的詳細資訊，請選取表格中的連結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2844">For more detailed information about EOP features, select the links in the table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-2845">提及 Exchange Online 時，通常是指 Office 365 企業版服務系列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2845">When Exchange Online is mentioned, it typically refers to the Office 365 Enterprise service family.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-2971"><sup>1</sup> 郵件使用者會定義為「信箱」，而且可以連同外部郵件連絡人直接在 Exchange 系統管理中心 (EAC) 中新增、移除或管理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2971"><sup>1</sup> Mail users are defined as "Mailboxes," and, along with external mail contacts, can be added, removed, and otherwise managed directly in the Exchange admin center (EAC).</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-2972"><sup>2</sup> 沒有 RBAC 自訂。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2972"><sup>2</sup> No RBAC customization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-2973">僅限系統管理員角色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2973">Admin roles only.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-2974"><sup>3</sup> 在 EAC 中，可檢視受管理網域和編輯網域類型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2974"><sup>3</sup> Managed domains can be viewed and domain types can be edited in the EAC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-2975">所有其他網域管理都必須在 Microsoft 365 系統管理中心完成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2975">All other domain management must be done in the Microsoft 365 admin center.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-2976">EOP 中的<sup>4 個</sup>郵件流程規則（也稱為傳輸規則）是在[Exchange Online Protection 中的郵件流程規則（傳輸規則）](https://docs.microsoft.com/microsoft-365/security/office-365-security/mail-flow-rules-transport-rules-0)中說明。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2976"><sup>4</sup> Mail flow rules (also known as transport rules) in EOP are described in [Mail flow rules (transport rules) in Exchange Online Protection](https://docs.microsoft.com/microsoft-365/security/office-365-security/mail-flow-rules-transport-rules-0).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-2977">EOP 與 Exchange Online 之間的可用郵件流程規則條件、例外狀況和動作略有不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2977">The available mail flow rule conditions, exceptions, and actions differ slightly between EOP and Exchange Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-2978">在 Exchange Online 中的[郵件流程規則條件和例外狀況（](https://docs.microsoft.com/Exchange/security-and-compliance/mail-flow-rules/conditions-and-exceptions)述詞）和[exchange Online 中的郵件流程規則動作](https://docs.microsoft.com/Exchange/security-and-compliance/mail-flow-rules/mail-flow-rule-actions)都有這些差異。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2978">These differences are noted in [Mail flow rule conditions and exceptions (predicates) in Exchange Online](https://docs.microsoft.com/Exchange/security-and-compliance/mail-flow-rules/conditions-and-exceptions) and [Mail flow rule actions in Exchange Online](https://docs.microsoft.com/Exchange/security-and-compliance/mail-flow-rules/mail-flow-rule-actions).</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-2979"><sup>5</sup> EOP 稽核報告是 Exchange Online 稽核報告的子集，但不包括信箱的相關資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2979"><sup>5</sup> EOP auditing reports are a subset of Exchange Online auditing reports that exclude information about mailboxes.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-2980"><sup>6</sup> DLP 原則祕訣不適用於 Exchange Enterprise CAL with Services 客戶。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2980"><sup>6</sup> DLP policy tips are not available for Exchange Enterprise CAL with Services customers.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-2981"><sup>7</sup> 預設的內容篩選動作，就是將垃圾郵件移至收件者的 [垃圾郵件] 資料夾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2981"><sup>7</sup> The default content filter action is to move spam messages to the recipients' Junk Email folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-2982">若要使用內部部署 Exchange 信箱，您也需要在內部部署 Exchange 組織中設定兩個傳輸規則，以偵測 EOP 新增的垃圾郵件頭。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2982">For this to work with on-premises Exchange mailboxes, you also need to configure two transport rules in your on-premises Exchange organization to detect spam headers added by EOP.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93edf-2983">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[確定垃圾郵件路由傳送至每個使用者的垃圾郵件資料夾](https://docs.microsoft.com/microsoft-365/security/office-365-security/ensure-that-spam-is-routed-to-each-user-s-junk-email-folder)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2983">For more information, see [Ensure that spam is routed to each user's Junk Email folder](https://docs.microsoft.com/microsoft-365/security/office-365-security/ensure-that-spam-is-routed-to-each-user-s-junk-email-folder).</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-2984"><sup>8</sup> 透過 EOP 篩選其信箱的 Exchange Server 2013 Service Pack 1 (SP1) 客戶可以使用此功能，而且很快就可以供 Exchange Online 客戶使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2984"><sup>8</sup> This feature is available to Exchange Server 2013 Service Pack 1 (SP1) customers whose mailboxes are being filtered by EOP, and will soon be available to Exchange Online customers.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-2985"><sup>9</sup> EOP 報告是 Exchange Online 報告的子集，但不包括信箱的相關資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2985"><sup>9</sup> EOP reports are a subset of Exchange Online reports that exclude information about mailboxes.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-2986"><sup>10</sup> 包括 DLP 報告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2986"><sup>10</sup> Includes DLP reports.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-2987"><sup>11</sup> Exchange Enterprise CAL with Services 客戶應該選取 **Exchange Online** 服務而非 **Exchange Online Protection** 服務，來安裝活頁簿。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2987"><sup>11</sup> Exchange Enterprise CAL with Services customers should install the workbook by selecting the **Exchange Online** service rather than the **Exchange Online Protection** service.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-2988"><sup>12</sup>對於購買 Azure 資訊保護並使用 Exchange online Protection 透過 exchange online 路由電子郵件的內部部署客戶提供支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2988"><sup>12</sup> Supported for on-premises customers who purchase Azure Information Protection and use Exchange Online Protection to route email through Exchange Online.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-2989"><sup>13</sup> 掃描輸入及輸出郵件，但未掃描從組織中寄件者傳送給組織中收件者的內部郵件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2989"><sup>13</sup> Scans inbound and outbound messages, but does not scan internal messages sent from a sender in your organization to a recipient in your organization.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-2990"><sup>14</sup> EOP 和 Exchange Online 之間可用的述詞和動作並不相同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2990"><sup>14</sup> The available predicates and actions differ between EOP and Exchange Online.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-2991"><sup>15</sup>混合式安裝程式不能透過混合式的嚮導使用，但如果您有 Exchange SP1，則可以手動設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2991"><sup>15</sup> Hybrid setup is not available through the Hybrid Wizard, but can be set up manually if you have Exchange SP1.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-2992"><sup>16</sup>可用於 Office 365 華東 E1 及更新版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2992"><sup>16</sup> Available in Office 365 Germany E1 and above.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-2993"><sup>17</sup>于 Office 365 德國 E3 中提供。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2993"><sup>17</sup> Available in Office 365 Germany E3.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="93edf-2994"><sup>18</sup>適用于 Office 365 德國的附加元件功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93edf-2994"><sup>18</sup> Available as an add-on feature for Office 365 Germany.</span></span>
